success sql.NullBool\\n276: \\n277: \\t// trying to obtain the lock with the specific name\\n278: \\t// the lock is exclusive per session and is released explicitly by executing RELEASE_LOCK() or db.Quote(\"sqlite_master\") + \" WHERE \" + db.Quote(\"type\") + \"='index' AND \" + db.Quote(\"tbl_name\") + \"=? AND \" + db.Quote(\"name\") + \"=?\"\n87: \treturn sql, args\n88: }\n89: \n90: func (db *SQLite3) ColumnCheckSQL(tableName, columnName string) (string, []any) {\n91: \t// Use PRAGMA table_info to check if a column exists on a table. In SQLite, quoting with backticks inside\n92: \t// pragma_table_info(<expr>) can be interpreted as an identifier/column. Instead, pass the table name as a\n93: \t// string literal to avoid ambiguity. We cannot parameterize identifiers, but pragma_table_info accepts string\n94: \t// literals, so we embed a single-quoted literal safely by replacing single quotes if any.\n95: \t// Note: tableName is expected to be a trusted identifier from migrations.\n96: \tsafeTable := strings.ReplaceAll(tableName, \"'\", \"''\")\n97: \tsql := \"SELECT 1 FROM pragma_table_info('\" + safeTable + \"') WHERE name = ?\"\n98: \treturn sql, []any{columnName}\n99: }\n100: \n101: func (db *SQLite3) DropIndexSQL(tableName string, index *Index) string {\n102: \tquote := db.Quote\n103: \t// var unique string\n104: \tidxName := index.XName(tableName)\n105: \treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"DROP INDEX %v\", quote(idxName))\n106: }\n107: \n108: func (db *SQLite3) CleanDB(engine *xorm.Engine) error {\n109: \treturn nil\n110: }\n111: \n112: // TruncateDBTables deletes all data from all the tables and resets the sequences.\n113: // A special case is the dashboard_acl table where we keep the default permissions.\n114: func (db *SQLite3) TruncateDBTables(engine *xorm.Engine) error {\n115: \ttables, err := engine.Dialect().GetTables()\n116: \tif err != nil {\n117: \t\treturn err\n118: \t}\n119: \n120: \tsess := engine.NewSession()\n121: \tdefer sess.Close()\n122: \n123: \tfor _, table := range tables {\n124: \t\tswitch table.Name {\n125: \t\tcase \"migration_log\":\n126: \t\t\tcontinue\n127: \t\tcase \"dashboard_acl\":\n128: \t\t\t// keep default dashboard permissions\n129: \t\t\tif _, err := sess.Exec(fmt.Sprintf(\"DELETE FROM %q WHERE dashboard_id != -1 AND org_id != -1;\", table.Name)); err != nil {\n130: \t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to truncate table %q: %w\", table.Name, err)\n131: \t\t\t}\n132: \t\t\tif _, err := sess.Exec(\"UPDATE sqlite_sequence SET seq = 2 WHERE name = '%s';\", table.Name); err != nil {\n133: \t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to cleanup sqlite_sequence: %w\", err)\n134: \t\t\t}\n135: \t\tdefault:\n136: \t\t\tif _, err := sess.Exec(fmt.Sprintf(\"DELETE FROM %s;\", table.Name)); err != nil {\n137: \t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to truncate table %q: %w\", table.Name, err)\n138: \t\t\t}\n139: \t\t}\n140: \t}\n141: \tif _, err := sess.Exec(\"UPDATE sqlite_sequence SET seq = 0 WHERE name != 'dashboard_acl';\"); err != nil {\n142: \t\t// if we have not created any autoincrement columns in the database this will fail, the error is expected and we can ignore it\n143: \t\t// we can't discriminate based on code because sqlite returns a generic error code\n144: \t\tif err.Error() != \"no such table: sqlite_sequence\" {\n145: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to cleanup sqlite_sequence: %w\", err)\n146: \t\t}\n147: \t}\n148: \treturn nil\n149: }\n150: \n151: func (db *SQLite3) ErrorMessage(err error) string {\n152: \treturn sqlite.ErrorMessage(err)\n153: }\n154: \n155: func (db *SQLite3) IsUniqueConstraintViolation(err error) bool {\n156: \treturn sqlite.IsUniqueConstraintViolation(err)\n157: }\n158: \n159: func (db *SQLite3) IsDeadlock(err error) bool {\n160: \treturn false // No deadlock\n161: }\n162: \n163: // UpsertSQL returns the upsert sql statement for SQLite dialect\n164: func (db *SQLite3) UpsertSQL(tableName string, keyCols, updateCols []string) string {\n165: \tstr, _ := db.UpsertMultipleSQL(tableName, keyCols, updateCols, 1)\n166: \treturn str\n167: }\n168: \n169: // UpsertMultipleSQL returns the upsert sql statement for PostgreSQL dialect\n170: func (db *SQLite3) UpsertMultipleSQL(tableName string, keyCols, updateCols []string, count int) (string, error) {\n171: \tif count < 1 {\n172: \t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"upsert statement must have count >= 1. Got %v\", count)\n173: \t}\n174: \tcolumnsStr := strings.Builder{}\n175: \tonConflictStr := strings.Builder{}\n176: \tcolPlaceHoldersStr := strings.Builder{}\n177: \tsetStr := strings.Builder{}\n178: \n179: \tconst separator = \", \"\n180: \tseparatorVar := separator\n181: \tfor i, c := range updateCols {\n182: \t\tif i == len(updateCols)-1 {\n183: \t\t\tseparatorVar = \"\"\n184: \t\t}\n185: \n186: \t\tcolumnsStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s%s\", db.Quote(c), separatorVar))\n187: \t\tcolPlaceHoldersStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"?%s\", separatorVar))\n188: \t\tsetStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s=excluded.%s%s\", db.Quote(c), db.Quote(c), separatorVar))\n189: \t}\n190: \n191: \tseparatorVar = separator\n192: \tfor i, c := range keyCols {\n193: \t\tif i == len(keyCols)-1 {\n194: \t\t\tseparatorVar = \"\"\n195: \t\t}\n196: \t\tonConflictStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s%s\", db.Quote(c), separatorVar))\n197: \t}\n198: \n199: \tvaluesStr := strings.Builder{}\n200: \tseparatorVar = separator\n201: \tcolPlaceHolders := colPlaceHoldersStr.String()\n202: \tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n203: \t\tif i == count-1 {\n204: \t\t\tseparatorVar = \"\"\n205: \t\t}\n206: \t\tvaluesStr.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"(%s)%s\", colPlaceHolders, separatorVar))\n207: \t}\n208: \n209: \ts := fmt.Sprintf(`INSERT INTO %s (%s) VALUES %s ON CONFLICT(%s) DO UPDATE SET %s`,\n210: \t\ttableName,\n211: \t\tcolumnsStr.String(),\n212: \t\tvaluesStr.String(),\n213: \t\tonConflictStr.String(),\n214: \t\tsetStr.String(),\n215: \t)\n216: \treturn s, nil\n217: }\n218: \n219: func (db *SQLite3) Concat(strs ...string) string {\n220: \treturn strings.Join(strs, \" || \")\n221: }\n222: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec@7b5876467dc156dd3117dd0b3c15f994100e9597/-/blob/pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/sqlite_dialect.go"}}}

'Migrator' struct in 'pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrator.go' is the core migration runner. It manages the entire migration lifecycle through the 'RunMigrations()' method, which:\\n- Loads previously executed migrations from the migration_log table\\n- Executes pending migrations in sequence within transactions\\n- Records each migration execution in the migration_log table\\n- Supports database-level locking via 'InTransaction()' method to prevent concurrent migrations\\n- Implements automatic retry logic for SQLite locked/busy errors\\n- Provides Prometheus metrics for migration performance tracking\\n\\n## Migration Version Tracking Table\\nThe migration_log table is automatically created by the Migrator and maintains a persistent record of all executed migrations. It includes columns for:\\n- id (auto-increment primary key)\\n- migration_id (unique identifier for each migration)\\n- sql (the SQL statement executed)\\n- success (boolean flag)\\n- error (error message if migration failed)\\n- timestamp (when the migration was executed)\\n\\nThis table is created in 'migrator.go' via the 'AddCreateMigration()' method and is queried by 'GetMigrationLog()' to determine which migrations have already been executed.\\n\\n## SQL Dialect Abstraction\\nThe framework provides comprehensive SQL dialect abstraction to support multiple databases:\\n\\n**Dialect Interface** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/dialect.go'): Defines the contract for database-specific implementations with methods for:\\n- SQL generation (CreateTableSQL, AddColumnSQL, DropIndexSQL, etc.)\\n- Type mapping (SQLType) for database-specific column types\\n- Quoting (Quote) identifiers appropriately for each database\\n- Database-specific operations (Lock/Unlock, IndexCheckSQL, ColumnCheckSQL)\\n- Upsert operations with dialect-specific syntax\\n\\n**MySQL Dialect** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/mysql_dialect.go'): Implements MySQLDialect with:\\n- InnoDB engine support with utf8mb4 charset\\n- Named locks using GET_LOCK() and RELEASE_LOCK()\\n- AUTO_INCREMENT primary keys\\n- ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE upsert syntax\\n- Error handling for MySQL-specific errors (duplicate key, deadlocks)\\n\\n**PostgreSQL Dialect** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/postgres_dialect.go'): Implements PostgresDialect with:\\n- Advisory locks using pg_try_advisory_lock() and pg_advisory_unlock()\\n- SERIAL auto-increment handling\\n- ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert syntax\\n- Error code handling via pq driver\\n- NULL ordering customization (NULLS FIRST/LAST)\\n\\n**SQLite Dialect** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/sqlite_dialect.go'): Implements SQLite3 with:\\n- AUTOINCREMENT support\\n- Smaller batch sizes (10) due to parameter count limits\\n- ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert syntax\\n- Index checks using sqlite_master table\\n- Column checks using PRAGMA table_info\\n\\n## Rollback Handling\\nThe framework implements rollback handling through:\\n1. **Transaction Wrapper**: The 'InTransaction()' method wraps all migration execution in database transactions (Begin/Commit/Rollback)\\n2. **Automatic Rollback**: If any migration fails during execution, the transaction is automatically rolled back via 'sess.Rollback()' in 'pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrator.go'\\n3. **Lock-based Atomicity**: Database-level locks (via dialect-specific Lock/Unlock implementations) ensure atomic migration execution across distributed systems\\n4. **Condition-based Execution**: Migration conditions ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/conditions.go') like 'IfColumnNotExistsCondition' and 'IfIndexNotExistsCondition' allow idempotent migrations that can be safely re-run\\n\\n## Migration Types\\nThe framework supports multiple migration types defined in 'pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrations.go':\\n- RawSQLMigration: Direct SQL execution with dialect-specific variants\\n- AddColumnMigration: Safe column addition with existence checks\\n- AddTableMigration: Table creation with proper key management\\n- DropTableMigration: Safe table removal\\n- AddIndexMigration: Index creation with existence checks\\n- DropIndexMigration: Index removal\\n- CodeMigration: Custom Go code execution within transaction context\\n- CopyTableDataMigration: Data migration between tables\\n\\nAll migration types inherit from MigrationBase and implement the Migration interface, which defines the contract for ID management, condition checking, and SQL generation via the dialect abstraction layer.\"\n   236→}\n 'pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/' and comprises the following key components:\\n\\n## Migration Runner\\nThe 'Migrator' struct in 'pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrator.go' is the core migration runner. It manages the entire migration lifecycle through the 'RunMigrations()' method, which:\\n- Loads previously executed migrations from the migration_log table\\n- Executes pending migrations in sequence within transactions\\n- Records each migration execution in the migration_log table\\n- Supports database-level locking via 'InTransaction()' method to prevent concurrent migrations\\n- Implements automatic retry logic for SQLite locked/busy errors\\n- Provides Prometheus metrics for migration performance tracking\\n\\n## Migration Version Tracking Table\\nThe migration_log table is automatically created by the Migrator and maintains a persistent record of all executed migrations. It includes columns for:\\n- id (auto-increment primary key)\\n- migration_id (unique identifier for each migration)\\n- sql (the SQL statement executed)\\n- success (boolean flag)\\n- error (error message if migration failed)\\n- timestamp (when the migration was executed)\\n\\nThis table is created in 'migrator.go' via the 'AddCreateMigration()' method and is queried by 'GetMigrationLog()' to determine which migrations have already been executed.\\n\\n## SQL Dialect Abstraction\\nThe framework provides comprehensive SQL dialect abstraction to support multiple databases:\\n\\n**Dialect Interface** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/dialect.go'): Defines the contract for database-specific implementations with methods for:\\n- SQL generation (CreateTableSQL, AddColumnSQL, DropIndexSQL, etc.)\\n- Type mapping (SQLType) for database-specific column types\\n- Quoting (Quote) identifiers appropriately for each database\\n- Database-specific operations (Lock/Unlock, IndexCheckSQL, ColumnCheckSQL)\\n- Upsert operations with dialect-specific syntax\\n\\n**MySQL Dialect** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/mysql_dialect.go'): Implements MySQLDialect with:\\n- InnoDB engine support with utf8mb4 charset\\n- Named locks using GET_LOCK() and RELEASE_LOCK()\\n- AUTO_INCREMENT primary keys\\n- ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE upsert syntax\\n- Error handling for MySQL-specific errors (duplicate key, deadlocks)\\n\\n**PostgreSQL Dialect** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/postgres_dialect.go'): Implements PostgresDialect with:\\n- Advisory locks using pg_try_advisory_lock() and pg_advisory_unlock()\\n- SERIAL auto-increment handling\\n- ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert syntax\\n- Error code handling via pq driver\\n- NULL ordering customization (NULLS FIRST/LAST)\\n\\n**SQLite Dialect** ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/sqlite_dialect.go'): Implements SQLite3 with:\\n- AUTOINCREMENT support\\n- Smaller batch sizes (10) due to parameter count limits\\n- ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert syntax\\n- Index checks using sqlite_master table\\n- Column checks using PRAGMA table_info\\n\\n## Rollback Handling\\nThe framework implements rollback handling through:\\n1. **Transaction Wrapper**: The 'InTransaction()' method wraps all migration execution in database transactions (Begin/Commit/Rollback)\\n2. **Automatic Rollback**: If any migration fails during execution, the transaction is automatically rolled back via 'sess.Rollback()' in 'pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrator.go'\\n3. **Lock-based Atomicity**: Database-level locks (via dialect-specific Lock/Unlock implementations) ensure atomic migration execution across distributed systems\\n4. **Condition-based Execution**: Migration conditions ('pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/conditions.go') like 'IfColumnNotExistsCondition' and 'IfIndexNotExistsCondition' allow idempotent migrations that can be safely re-run\\n\\n## Migration Types\\nThe framework supports multiple migration types defined in 'pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrations.go':\\n- RawSQLMigration: Direct SQL execution with dialect-specific variants\\n- AddColumnMigration: Safe column addition with existence checks\\n- AddTableMigration: Table creation with proper key management\\n- DropTableMigration: Safe table removal\\n- AddIndexMigration: Index creation with existence checks\\n- DropIndexMigration: Index removal\\n- CodeMigration: Custom Go code execution within transaction context\\n- CopyTableDataMigration: Data migration between tables\\n\\nAll migration types inherit from MigrationBase and implement the Migration interface, which defines the contract for ID management, condition checking, and SQL generation via the dialect abstraction layer.\"\n}\n","numLines":237,"startLine":1,"totalLines":237}}}
